```
export interface Input {

}
```

   147	const [getBindings] = createProgramState(() => new Set<Binding>());
   148	const [getNextBindingId, setNextBindingId] = createProgramState(() => 0);
   149	export function createBinding(
   150	  name: string,
   151	  type: Binding["type"],
   152	  section: Section,
   153	  upstreamAlias?: Binding["upstreamAlias"],
   154	  property?: string,
   155	  excludeProperties?: Opt<string>,
   156	  loc: t.SourceLocation | null = null,
   157	  declared = false,
   158	): Binding {
   159	  const id = getNextBindingId();
   160	  const binding: Binding = {
   161	    id,
   162	    name,
   163	    type,
   164	    loc,
   165	    section,
   166	    property,
   167	    declared,
   168	    closureSections: undefined,
   169	    assignmentSections: undefined,
   170	    excludeProperties,
   171	    sources: undefined,
   172	    aliases: new Set(),
   173	    hoists: new Map(),
   174	    propertyAliases: new Map(),
   175	    upstreamAlias,
   176	    downstreamExpressions: new Set(),
   177	    scopeOffset: undefined,
   178	    export: undefined,
   179	    nullable: excludeProperties === undefined,
   180	  };
   181	
   182	  if (property) {
   183	    if (declared) upstreamAlias!.nullable = false;
   184	    // TODO: should prefer declared properties as alias roots.
   185	    const propBinding = upstreamAlias!.propertyAliases.get(property);
   186	    if (propBinding) {
   187	      binding.property = undefined;
   188	      binding.upstreamAlias = propBinding;
   189	      propBinding.aliases.add(binding);
   190	    } else {
   191	      // TODO: check if default is used, if so an intermediate binding is needed
   192	      upstreamAlias!.propertyAliases.set(property, binding);
   193	    }
   194	  } else if (upstreamAlias) {
   195	    upstreamAlias.aliases.add(binding);
   196	  }
   197	
   198	  setNextBindingId(id + 1);
   199	  getBindings().add(binding);
   200	  return binding;
   201	}

   203	export function trackVarReferences(
   204	  tag: t.NodePath<t.MarkoTag>,
   205	  type: BindingType,
   206	  upstreamAlias?: Binding["upstreamAlias"],
   207	) {
   208	  const tagVar = tag.node.var;
   209	  if (tagVar) {
   210	    let canonicalUpstreamAlias = getCanonicalBinding(upstreamAlias);
   211	    if (canonicalUpstreamAlias) {
   212	      const { excludeProperties } = canonicalUpstreamAlias;
   213	      if (excludeProperties !== undefined) {
   214	        canonicalUpstreamAlias = canonicalUpstreamAlias.upstreamAlias!;
   215	      }
   216	      createBindingsAndTrackReferences(
   217	        tagVar,
   218	        canonicalUpstreamAlias.type,
   219	        tag.scope,
   220	        canonicalUpstreamAlias.section,
   221	        canonicalUpstreamAlias,
   222	        undefined,
   223	        excludeProperties,
   224	      );
   225	      return canonicalUpstreamAlias;
   226	    }
   227	
   228	    createBindingsAndTrackReferences(
   229	      tagVar,
   230	      type,
   231	      tag.scope,
   232	      getOrCreateSection(tag),
   233	      undefined,
   234	      undefined,
   235	      undefined,
   236	    );
   237	    return tagVar.extra?.binding;
   238	  }
   239	}
   240	
   241	export function trackParamsReferences(
   242	  body: t.NodePath<t.MarkoTagBody | t.Program>,
   243	  type: BindingType,
   244	  upstreamAlias?: Binding["upstreamAlias"],
   245	) {
   246	  const params = body.node.params;
   247	  if (body.node.body.length && params.length) {
   248	    const canonicalUpstreamAlias = getCanonicalBinding(upstreamAlias);
   249	    let section: Section;
   250	    if (canonicalUpstreamAlias) {
   251	      section = canonicalUpstreamAlias.section;
   252	      type = canonicalUpstreamAlias.type;
   253	    } else {
   254	      section = getOrCreateSection(body);
   255	    }
   256	    const paramsBinding =
   257	      canonicalUpstreamAlias ||
   258	      ((body.node.extra ??= {}).binding = createBinding(
   259	        generateUid("params"),
   260	        type,
   261	        section,
   262	        undefined,
   263	        undefined,
   264	      ));
   265	
   266	    section.params = paramsBinding;
   267	
   268	    for (let i = 0; i < params.length; i++) {
   269	      const param = params[i];
   270	      if (param.type === "RestElement") {
   271	        createBindingsAndTrackReferences(
   272	          param.argument,
   273	          type,
   274	          body.scope,
   275	          section,
   276	          paramsBinding,
   277	          undefined,
   278	          addNumericPropertiesUntil(undefined, i - 1),
   279	        );
   280	      } else if (t.isLVal(param)) {
   281	        createBindingsAndTrackReferences(
   282	          param,
   283	          type,
   284	          body.scope,
   285	          section,
   286	          paramsBinding,
   287	          i + "",
   288	          undefined,
   289	        );
   290	      }
   291	    }
   292	
   293	    return paramsBinding;
   294	  }
   295	}
   296	
   297	export function trackHoistedReference(
   298	  referencePath: t.NodePath<t.Identifier>,
   299	  binding: Binding,
   300	) {
   301	  const section = binding.section;
   302	  const referenceSection = getOrCreateSection(referencePath);
   303	  const hoistSection = getCommonSection(referenceSection, section);
   304	  const extra = (referencePath.node.extra ??= {});
   305	
   306	  let hoistedBinding = binding.hoists.get(hoistSection);
   307	  if (!hoistedBinding) {
   308	    binding.hoists.set(
   309	      hoistSection,
   310	      (hoistedBinding = createBinding(
   311	        generateUid("hoisted_" + referencePath.node.name),
   312	        BindingType.hoist,
   313	        hoistSection,
   314	        undefined,
   315	        undefined,
   316	        undefined,
   317	        binding.loc,
   318	        true,
   319	      )),
   320	    );
   321	
   322	    section.hoisted = bindingUtil.add(section.hoisted, binding);
   323	
   324	    let currentSection = section.parent;
   325	    while (currentSection && currentSection !== hoistSection) {
   326	      currentSection.isHoistThrough = true;
   327	      currentSection = currentSection.parent;
   328	    }
   329	  }
   330	
   331	  if (isInvokedFunction(referencePath)) {
   332	    extra.read = createRead(hoistedBinding, undefined);
   333	    extra.section = referenceSection;
   334	    extra[kIsInvoked] = true;
   335	  } else {
   336	    trackReference(referencePath, hoistedBinding);
   337	  }
   338	
   339	  referenceSection.referencedHoists = bindingUtil.add(
   340	    referenceSection.referencedHoists,
   341	    hoistedBinding,
   342	  );
   343	}
   344	
   345	function trackReferencesForBinding(babelBinding: t.Binding, binding: Binding) {
   346	  const { referencePaths, constantViolations } = babelBinding;
   347	
   348	  for (const referencePath of referencePaths) {
   349	    const referenceSection = getOrCreateSection(referencePath);
   350	    if (isSameOrChildSection(binding.section, referenceSection)) {
   351	      if (
   352	        binding.type === BindingType.local &&
   353	        referenceSection === binding.section
   354	      ) {
   355	        continue;
   356	      }
   357	      trackReference(referencePath as t.NodePath<t.Identifier>, binding);
   358	    } else {
   359	      trackHoistedReference(referencePath as t.NodePath<t.Identifier>, binding);
   360	    }
   361	  }
   362	
   363	  for (const ref of constantViolations) {
   364	    if (ref.isUpdateExpression()) {
   365	      trackAssignment(ref.get("argument"), binding);
   366	    } else if (ref.isAssignmentExpression()) {
   367	      trackAssignment(ref.get("left"), binding);
   368	
   369	      if (ref.node.operator !== "=") {
   370	        /*
   371	         * https://github.com/babel/babel/issues/11313
   372	         * We need this so we can handle `+=` and friends
   373	         */
   374	        const left = ref.get("left");
   375	        if (left.isIdentifier()) {
   376	          trackReference(left, binding);
   377	        }
   378	      }
   379	    }
   380	  }
   381	}
   382	
   383	function trackAssignment(
   384	  assignment: t.NodePath<
   385	    t.AssignmentExpression["left"] | t.UpdateExpression["argument"]
   386	  >,
   387	  binding: Binding,
   388	) {
   389	  const fnRoot = getFnRoot(assignment);
   390	  const fnExtra = fnRoot && ((fnRoot.node.extra ??= {}) as FnExtra);
   391	  const section = getOrCreateSection(assignment);
   392	  setReferencesScope(assignment);
   393	  forEachIdentifierPath(assignment, (id) => {
   394	    if (id.node.name === binding.name) {
   395	      const extra = (id.node.extra ??= {}) as AssignedBindingExtra;
   396	
   397	      if (binding.upstreamAlias && binding.property !== undefined) {
   398	        const changePropName = binding.property + "Change";
   399	        const changeBinding =
   400	          binding.upstreamAlias.propertyAliases.get(changePropName) ||
   401	          createBinding(
   402	            generateUid(changePropName),
   403	            BindingType.derived,
   404	            binding.section,
   405	            binding.upstreamAlias,
   406	            changePropName,
   407	            undefined,
   408	            id.node.loc,
   409	            true,
   410	          );
   411	        extra.assignmentTo = changeBinding;
   412	        addReadToExpression(id, changeBinding);
   413	      }
   414	
   415	      binding.assignmentSections = sectionUtil.add(
   416	        binding.assignmentSections,
   417	        section,
   418	      );
   419	      extra.assignment = binding;
   420	      extra.section = section;
   421	      extra.fnExtra = fnExtra;
   422	    }
   423	  });
   424	}
   425	
   426	export function setReferencesScope(path: t.NodePath<any>) {
   427	  const fnRoot = getFnRoot(path);
   428	  if (fnRoot) {
   429	    (fnRoot.node.extra ??= {}).referencesScope = true;
   430	  }
   431	}
   432	
   433	function createBindingsAndTrackReferences(
   434	  lVal: t.LVal,
   435	  type: BindingType,
   436	  scope: t.Scope,
   437	  section: Section,
   438	  upstreamAlias: Binding["upstreamAlias"] | undefined,
   439	  property: string | undefined,
   440	  excludeProperties: Opt<string>,
   441	) {
   442	  switch (lVal.type) {
   443	    case "Identifier":
   444	      trackReferencesForBinding(
   445	        scope.getBinding(lVal.name)!,
   446	        ((lVal.extra ??= {}).binding = createBinding(
   447	          lVal.name,
   448	          type,
   449	          section,
   450	          upstreamAlias,
   451	          property,
   452	          excludeProperties,
   453	          lVal.loc,
   454	          true,
   455	        )),
   456	      );
   457	      break;
   458	    case "ObjectPattern": {
   459	      const patternBinding =
   460	        (property
   461	          ? upstreamAlias!.propertyAliases.get(property)
   462	          : upstreamAlias) ||
   463	        ((lVal.extra ??= {}).binding = createBinding(
   464	          generateUid(property || "pattern"),
   465	          type,
   466	          section,
   467	          upstreamAlias,
   468	          property,
   469	          excludeProperties,
   470	          lVal.loc,
   471	        ));
   472	
   473	      const hasRest =
   474	        lVal.properties[lVal.properties.length - 1]?.type === "RestElement";
   475	      for (const prop of lVal.properties) {
   476	        if (prop.type === "RestElement") {
   477	          createBindingsAndTrackReferences(
   478	            prop.argument,
   479	            type,
   480	            scope,
   481	            section,
   482	            patternBinding,
   483	            property,
   484	            excludeProperties,
   485	          );
   486	        } else {
   487	          let key: string;
   488	
   489	          if (prop.key.type === "Identifier") {
   490	            key = prop.key.name;
   491	          } else if (prop.key.type === "StringLiteral") {
   492	            key = prop.key.value;
   493	          } else {
   494	            // TODO: it should be a computed value
   495	            throw new Error("computed keys not supported in object pattern");
   496	          }
   497	
   498	          if (hasRest) {
   499	            excludeProperties = propsUtil.add(excludeProperties, key);
   500	          }
   501	
   502	          if (t.isLVal(prop.value)) {
   503	            createBindingsAndTrackReferences(
   504	              prop.value,
   505	              type,
   506	              scope,
   507	              section,
   508	              patternBinding,
   509	              key,
   510	              undefined,
   511	            );
   512	          }
   513	        }
   514	      }
   515	      break;
   516	    }
   517	    case "ArrayPattern": {
   518	      const patternBinding =
   519	        (property
   520	          ? upstreamAlias!.propertyAliases.get(property)
   521	          : upstreamAlias) ||
   522	        ((lVal.extra ??= {}).binding = createBinding(
   523	          generateUid(property || "pattern"),
   524	          type,
   525	          section,
   526	          upstreamAlias,
   527	          property,
   528	          excludeProperties,
   529	          lVal.loc,
   530	        ));
   531	
   532	      let i = -1;
   533	      for (const element of lVal.elements) {
   534	        i++;
   535	        if (element) {
   536	          if (element.type === "RestElement") {
   537	            excludeProperties = addNumericPropertiesUntil(
   538	              excludeProperties,
   539	              i - 1,
   540	            );
   541	            createBindingsAndTrackReferences(
   542	              element.argument,
   543	              type,
   544	              scope,
   545	              section,
   546	              patternBinding,
   547	              property,
   548	              excludeProperties,
   549	            );
   550	          } else if (t.isLVal(element)) {
   551	            createBindingsAndTrackReferences(
   552	              element,
   553	              type,
   554	              scope,
   555	              section,
   556	              patternBinding,
   557	              `${i}`,
   558	              undefined,
   559	            );
   560	          }
   561	        }
   562	      }
   563	      break;
   564	    }
   565	    case "AssignmentPattern":
   566	      // TODO: this makes a default value an alias,
   567	      // but it really should be a computed value
   568	      createBindingsAndTrackReferences(
   569	        lVal.left,
   570	        type,
   571	        scope,
   572	        section,
   573	        upstreamAlias,
   574	        property,
   575	        undefined,
   576	      );
   577	
   578	      if (lVal.left.extra?.binding) {
   579	        (lVal.right.extra ??= {}).downstream = {
   580	          bindings: lVal.left.extra.binding,
   581	          excludeProperties: undefined,
   582	        };
   583	      }
   584	      break;
   585	  }
   586	}
   587

   591	) {
   592	  let root: t.NodePath<t.Identifier> | t.NodePath<t.MemberExpressio<response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you.     24	    assertNoParams(tag);
    25	    assertNoBodyContent(tag);

    27	    const [valueAttr] = node.attributes;
    28	
    29	    if (!node.var) {
    30	      throw tag
    31	        .get("name")
    32	        .buildCodeFrameError("The `const` tag requires a tag variable.");
    33	    }
    34	
    35	    if (!valueAttr) {
    36	      throw tag
    37	        .get("name")
    38	        .buildCodeFrameError("The `const` tag requires a value.");
    39	    }
    40	
    41	    if (
    42	      node.attributes.length > 1 ||
    43	      !t.isMarkoAttribute(valueAttr) ||
    44	      (!valueAttr.default && valueAttr.name !== "value")
    45	    ) {
    46	      throw tag
    47	        .get("name")
    48	        .buildCodeFrameError(
    49	          "The `const` tag only supports the `value` attribute.",
    50	        );
    51	    }
    52	
    53	    const valueExtra = evaluate(valueAttr.value);
    54	    const upstreamAlias = t.isIdentifier(valueAttr.value)
    55	      ? tag.scope.getBinding(valueAttr.value.name)?.identifier.extra?.binding
    56	      : undefined;
    57	
    58	    if (upstreamAlias) {
    59	      valueExtra.pruned = true;
    60	    }
    61	
    62	    const binding = trackVarReferences(tag, BindingType.derived, upstreamAlias);
    63	
    64	    if (binding) {
    65	      if (!valueExtra.nullable) binding.nullable = false;
    66	      setBindingValueExpr(binding, valueExtra);
    67	      valueExtra.downstream = {
    68	        bindings: binding,
    69	        excludeProperties: undefined,
    70	      };
    71	    }
    72	  },

    76	      const [valueAttr] = node.attributes;
    77	      const { value } = valueAttr;
    78

     2	import {
     3	  assertNoArgs,
     4	  assertNoParams,
     5	  computeNode,
     6	  type Tag,
     7	} from "@marko/compiler/babel-utils";
     8	
     9	import { assertNoBodyContent, assertNoSpreadAttrs } from "../util/assert";
    10	import { getAccessorPrefix } from "../util/get-accessor-char";
    11	import { isOutputDOM } from "../util/marko-config";
    12	import {
    13	  BindingType,
    14	  mergeReferences,
    15	  setBindingValueExpr,
    16	  trackVarReferences,
    17	} from "../util/references";
    18	import runtimeInfo from "../util/runtime-info";
    19	import { getScopeExpression } from "../util/scope-read";
    20	import { getOrCreateSection, getSection } from "../util/sections";
    21	import { forceBindingSerialize } from "../util/serialize-reasons";
    22	import {
    23	  addValue,
    24	  initValue,
    25	  setBindingSerializedValue,
    26	} from "../util/signals";
    27	import translateVar from "../util/translate-var";
    28	
    29	declare module "@marko/compiler/dist/types" {
    30	  export interface NodeExtra {
    31	    static?: boolean;
    32	  }
    33	}
    34	
    35	export default {
    36	  analyze(tag: t.NodePath<t.MarkoTag>) {
    37	    const { node } = tag;
    38	    const tagVar = node.var;
    39	    let valueAttr: t.MarkoAttribute | undefined;
    40	    let valueChangeAttr: t.MarkoAttribute | undefined;
    41	    for (const attr of node.attributes) {
    42	      if (t.isMarkoAttribute(attr)) {
    43	        if (attr.name === "value") {
    44	          valueAttr = attr;
    45	        } else if (attr.name === "valueChange") {
    46	          valueChangeAttr = attr;
    47	        } else {
    48	          const start = attr.loc?.start;
    49	          const end = attr.loc?.end;
    50	          const msg =
    51	            "The `let` tag only supports the `value` attribute and its change handler.";
    52	
    53	          if (start == null || end == null) {
    54	            throw tag.get("name").buildCodeFrameError(msg);
    55	          } else {
    56	            throw tag.hub.buildError(
    57	              { loc: { start, end } } as unknown as t.Node,
    58	              msg,
    59	              Error,
    60	            );
    61	          }
    62	        }
    63	      }
    64	    }
    65	
    66	    assertNoArgs(tag);
    67	    assertNoParams(tag);
    68	    assertNoBodyContent(tag);
    69	    assertNoSpreadAttrs(tag);
    70	
    71	    if (!tagVar) {
    72	      throw tag
    73	        .get("name")
    74	        .buildCodeFrameError("The `let` tag requires a tag variable.");
    75	    }
    76	
    77	    if (!t.isIdentifier(tagVar)) {
    78	      throw tag
    79	        .get("var")
    80	        .buildCodeFrameError("The `let` tag variable cannot be destructured.");
    81	    }
    82	
    83	    if (valueChangeAttr && computeNode(valueChangeAttr.value)) {
    84	      throw tag
    85	        .get("attributes")
    86	        .find((attr) => attr.node === valueChangeAttr)!
    87	        .get("value")
    88	        .buildCodeFrameError(
    89	          "The `let` tag `valueChange` attribute must be a function.",
    90	        );
    91	    }
    92	
    93	    const tagSection = getOrCreateSection(tag);
    94	    const binding = trackVarReferences(tag, BindingType.let)!;
    95	    setBindingValueExpr(
    96	      binding,
    97	      mergeReferences(tagSection, tag.node, [
    98	        valueAttr?.value,
    99	        valueChangeAttr?.value,
   100	      ]),
   101	    );
   102	
   103	    if (valueChangeAttr) {
   104	      // TODO: could be based on if there are actually assignments.
   105	      forceBindingSerialize(
   106	        tagSection,
   107	        binding,
   108	        getAccessorPrefix().TagVariableChange,
   109	      );
   110	    }
   111	  },
   112	  translate: {
   113	    exit(tag) {
   114	      const { node } = tag;
   115	      const tagVar = node.var!;
   116	      const valueAttr =
   117	        node.attributes.find(
   118	          (attr) =>
   119	            t.isMarkoAttribute(attr) && (attr.default || attr.name === "value"),
   120	        ) ?? t.markoAttribute("value", t.identifier("undefined"));
   121	      const valueChangeAttr = node.attributes.find(
   122	        (attr) => t.isMarkoAttribute(attr) && attr.name === "valueChange",
   123	      );
   124	      const section = getSection(tag);
   125	      const binding = tagVar.extra!.binding!;
   126	
   127	      if (isOutputDOM()) {
   128	        const signal = initValue(binding, "state");
   129	        const referencedBindings = tag.node.extra!.referencedBindings;
   130	
   131	        addValue(section, referencedBindings, signal, valueAttr.value);
   132	
   133	        if (valueChangeAttr) {
   134	          signal.extraArgs = [valueChangeAttr.value];
   135	        }
   136	
   137	        signal.buildAssignment = (valueSection, value) => {
   138	          const scope = getScopeExpression(valueSection, signal.section);
   139	
   140	          return t.callExpression(signal.identifier, [scope, value]);
   141	        };
   142	      } else {
   143	        translateVar(tag, valueAttr.value, "let");
   144	
   145	        if (valueChangeAttr) {
   146	          setBindingSerializedValue(
   147	            section,
   148	            binding,
   149	            valueChangeAttr.value,
   150	            getAccessorPrefix().TagVariableChange,
   151	          );
   152	        }
   153	      }
   154	
   155	      tag.remove();
   156	    },
   157	  },
   158	  parseOptions: {
   159	    openTagOnly: true,
   160	  },
   161	  attributes: {},
   162	  autocomplete: [
   163	    {
   164	      description: "Use to create a mutable binding.",
   165	      descriptionMoreURL: "https://markojs.com/docs/core-tags/#let",
   166	    },
   167	  ],
   168	  types: runtimeInfo.name + "/tags/let.d.marko",
   169	} as Tag;

+        ? markoRoot.node.default
+          ? t.toIdentifier(
+              markoRoot.parentPath.has("var")
+                ? markoRoot.parentPath.get("var")
+                : markoRoot.parentPath.get("name"),
+            )
+          : markoRoot.node.name
+        : t.isVariableDeclarator(fn.parent) && t.isIdentifier(fn.parent.id)
+          ? fn.parent.id.name
+          : t.isObjectMethod(node) && t.isIdentifier(node.key)
+            ? node.key.name
+            : "anonymous");

+    if (markoRoot.isMarkoScriptlet()) {
+      const refs = getStaticDeclRefs(fnExtra, fn);
+      if (refs === true) {
+        registerFunction(fnExtra);
+      } else if (refs.size) {
+        getReferencesByFn().set(fnExtra, refs);
+      }
+    } else if (shouldAlwaysRegister(markoRoot)) {
+      registerFunction(fnExtra);
+    } else {
+      getReferencesByFn().set(fnExtra, new Set([(exprRoot.node.extra ??= {})]));
+    }
+  },

+export function finalizeFunctionRegistry() {
+  for (const [fnExtra, exprExtras] of getReferencesByFn()) {
+    const seenExtras = new Set<t.NodeExtra>();
+    let shouldRegister = false;
+    for (const exprExtra of exprExtras) {
+      const refExtra = getCanonicalExtra(exprExtra);
+      if (seenExtras.has(refExtra)) continue;
+      seenExtras.add(refExtra);

+      if (couldSerializeDownstream(refExtra.downstream)) {

+function couldSerializeDownstream(downstream: t.NodeExtra["downstream"]) {
+  if (downstream) {
+    return Array.isArray(downstream.bindings)
+      ? downstream.bindings.some((binding) => couldSerializeBinding(binding))
+      : couldSerializeBinding(
+          downstream.bindings,
+          downstream.excludeProperties,
+        );
+  }
+
+  return false;
+}
+
+function couldSerializeBinding(
+  binding: Binding,
+  excludeProperties?: Set<string> | undefined,
+) {
+  if (getBindingSerializeReason(binding.section, binding)) {
+    return true;
+  }
+
+  for (const expr of binding.downstreamExpressions) {
+    if (expr.isEffect || couldSerializeDownstream(expr.downstream)) {
+      return true;
+    }
+  }

-      isMarkoAttribute(markoRoot) &&
-      ((isNativeTag(markoRoot.parentPath) &&

+      return true;
+    }
+  }
+
+  for (const [name, propBinding] of binding.propertyAliases) {
+    if (!excludeProperties?.has(name) && couldSerializeBinding(propBinding)) {
+      return true;
+    }
+  }
+
+  return false;
+}
+
+function canIgnoreRegister(
+  markoRoot: MarkoExprRootPath,
+  exprRoot: t.NodePath<t.Node>,
+) {
+  return (

         /^on[A-Z-]/.test(markoRoot.node.name)) ||
         isCoreTagName(markoRoot.parentPath, "script") ||

-        isCoreTagName(markoRoot.parentPath, "for"))

-      // Native tags, effects, lifecycles, and for loops aren't registered here since handle pulling in the function themselves.
-      return;
+        isCoreTagName(markoRoot.parentPath, "for")))
+  );

+function shouldAlwaysRegister(markoRoot: MarkoExprRootPath) {
+  const tag = getTagFromMarkoRoot(markoRoot);
+  if (!tag) return false;
+  if (isCoreTagName(tag, "let")) return true;
+  if (isCoreTagName(tag, "return")) return true;
+
+  switch (analyzeTagNameType(tag)) {
+    case TagNameType.DynamicTag:
+    case TagNameType.NativeTag:
+      // Passing a function to a dynamic tag could always be potentially serialized.
+      // Native tag event handlers are skipped in the `canIgnoreRegister`
+      // if it's anything else we need to unconditionally serialize.
+      return true;
+    case TagNameType.AttributeTag:
+      if (
+        analyzeTagNameType(getAttributeTagParent(tag)) ===
+        TagNameType.DynamicTag
+      ) {
+        return true;
+      }
+      break;
+  }
+
+  return false;
+}
+
+function getTagFromMarkoRoot(
+  markoRoot: MarkoExprRootPath,
+): t.NodePath<t.MarkoTag> | undefined {
+  let cur = markoRoot;
+  do {
+    if (cur.isMarkoTag()) return cur;
+    cur = cur.parentPath as MarkoExprRootPath;
+  } while (cur);
+}
+
+function registerFunction(fnExtra: RegisteredFnExtra) {
+  const {
+    markoOpts,
+    path: program,
+    opts: { filename },
+  } = getFile();
+  program.node.extra.isInteractive = true;
+  fnExtra.name = generateUid(fnExtra.name);
+  fnExtra.registerId = getTemplateId(
+    markoOpts,
+    filename as string,
+    `${fnExtra.section.id}/${fnExtra.name.slice(1)}`,
+  );

import { types as t } from "@marko/compiler";
import {
  getFile,
  getProgram,
  getTemplateId,
  isNativeTag,
} from "@marko/compiler/babel-utils";

import { generateUid } from "../util/generate-uid";
import { getFnRoot, getMarkoRoot } from "../util/get-root";
import { isCoreTagName } from "../util/is-core-tag";
import { getSection } from "../util/sections";
import type { TemplateVisitor } from "../util/visitors";
declare module "@marko/compiler/dist/types" {
  export interface FunctionDeclarationExtra {
    registerId?: string;
    name?: string;
  }

  export interface FunctionExpressionExtra {
    registerId?: string;
    name?: string;
  }

  export interface ArrowFunctionExpressionExtra {
    registerId?: string;
    name?: string;
  }
}

export default {
  analyze(fn) {
    if (fn !== getFnRoot(fn)) {
      return;
    }

    const markoRoot = getMarkoRoot(fn);
    if (
      markoRoot &&
      (markoRoot.isMarkoPlaceholder() ||
        (markoRoot.isMarkoScriptlet() && markoRoot.node.target === "server"))
    ) {
      // Server only or render only functions never need to be registered.
      return;
    }

    if (
      isMarkoAttribute(markoRoot) &&
      ((isNativeTag(markoRoot.parentPath) &&
        /^on[A-Z-]/.test(markoRoot.node.name)) ||
        isCoreTagName(markoRoot.parentPath, "script") ||
        isCoreTagName(markoRoot.parentPath, "lifecycle") ||
        isCoreTagName(markoRoot.parentPath, "for"))
    ) {
      // Native tags, effects, lifecycles, and for loops aren't registered here since handle pulling in the function themselves.
      return;
    }

    const { node } = fn;
    const section = getSection(fn);
    const extra = (node.extra ??= {});
    const {
      markoOpts,
      opts: { filename },
    } = getFile();
    const name = (extra.name = generateUid(
      (fn.node as t.FunctionExpression).id?.name ||
        (isMarkoAttribute(markoRoot)
          ? markoRoot.node.default
            ? t.toIdentifier(
                markoRoot.parentPath.has("var")
                  ? markoRoot.parentPath.get("var")
                  : markoRoot.parentPath.get("name"),
              )
            : markoRoot.node.name
          : t.isVariableDeclarator(fn.parent) && t.isIdentifier(fn.parent.id)
            ? fn.parent.id.name
            : t.isObjectMethod(node) && t.isIdentifier(node.key)
              ? node.key.name
              : "anonymous"),
    ));

    extra.section = section;
    extra.registerId = getTemplateId(
      markoOpts,
      filename as string,
      `${section.id}/${name.slice(1)}`,
    );

    getProgram().node.extra.isInteractive = true;
  },
} satisfies TemplateVisitor<t.Function>;

function isMarkoAttribute(
  path: t.NodePath | undefined | null,
): path is t.NodePath<t.MarkoAttribute> & {
  parent: t.MarkoTag;
  parentPath: t.NodePath<t.MarkoTag>;
} {
  return path ? path.isMarkoAttribute() : false;



2025-12-27 00:47:59,841 - INFO - swea-agent-marko-js__marko-2793 - ========================= STEP 52 =========================
2025-12-27 00:47:59,847 - DEBUG - swea-lm-marko-js__marko-2793 - n_cache_control: 2
2025-12-27 00:48:13,691 - DEBUG - swea-lm-marko-js__marko-2793 - Response: ChatCompletion(id='msg_017b8nB19gFnfQgZTdxEdyeK', choices=[Choice(finish_reason='tool_calls', index=0, logprobs=None, message=ChatCompletionMessage(content='I see! In version 6.0.55, ALL functions that passed the checks were registered. But in version 6.0.56, the function registration was changed to be more selective - it only registers functions when they could potentially be serialized.\n\nLooking at the new code in 6.0.56, there\'s a `shouldAlwaysRegister` function that checks if a function should always be registered:\n\n```typescript\nfunction shouldAlwaysRegister(markoRoot: MarkoExprRootPath) {\n  const tag = getTagFromMarkoRoot(markoRoot);\n  if (!tag) return false;\n  if (isCoreTagName(tag, "let")) return true;  // <--- This line!\n  if (isCoreTagName(tag, "return")) return true;\n  ...\n}\n```\n\nThe issue is that when a function is defined within a `<const>` tag, the function needs to be registered because it may reference `<let>` variables that can be assigned. I see! In version 6.0.55, ALL functions that passed the checks were registered. But in version 6.0.56, the function registration was changed to be more selective - it only registers functions when they could potentially be serialized.

Looking at the new code in 6.0.56, there's a `shouldAlwaysRegister` function that checks if a function should always be registered:

```typescript
function shouldAlwaysRegister(markoRoot: MarkoExprRootPath) {
  const tag = getTagFromMarkoRoot(markoRoot);
  if (!tag) return false;
  if (isCoreTagName(tag, "let")) return true;  // <--- This line!
  if (isCoreTagName(tag, "return")) return true;
  ...
}
```

The issue is that when a function is defined within a `<const>` tag, the function needs to be registered because it may reference `<let>` variables that can be assigned. The fix from 6.0.55 to 6.0.56 added this check for `<let>` tags but it seems like it's only checking if the function is directly in a `<let>` tag, not if it's in a `<const>` tag that might assign to a `<let>` variable.

So the issue is that `<const>` tags create bindings with `BindingType.derived`, which should be read-only, whereas `<let>` tags create bindings with `BindingType.let`, which can be mutated. 

Looking at the PR description more carefully, the issue is that within a function defined by a `<const>` tag, an assignment is made to a `<let>` variable. The problem introduced in 6.0.56 is that the function registry now checks whether functions need to be registered based on whether they could be serialized. The logic should handle the case where a function defined in a `<const>` tag assigns to a `<let>` variable.

Let me trace through the logic:

1. A `<let>` tag defines a mutable `timer` variable with `BindingType.let`
2. A `<const>` tag defines a function `reset` that assigns to `timer`
3. The function needs to be registered because it references a stateful binding

The issue in 6.0.56 is in the `shouldAlwaysRegister` function. It returns `true` for functions directly in `<let>` tags, but not for functions in `<const>` tags. However, a function in a `<const>` tag should also be registered if it assigns to a `<let>` variable.

export default function translateVar(
  tag: t.NodePath<t.MarkoTag>,
  initialValue: t.Expression,
  kind: "let" | "const" = "const",
) {
  const {
    node: { var: tagVar },
  } = tag;

  if (!tagVar) {
    return;
  }

  forEachIdentifierPath(tag.get("var"), (id) => {
    const binding = id.node.extra?.binding;
    if (
      !binding ||
      !binding.upstreamAlias ||
      !binding.assignmentSections ||
      id.node === tagVar
    ) {
      return;
    }

    const changeName = binding.name + "Change";
    const changeBinding = binding.upstreamAlias.propertyAliases.get(changeName);
    if (changeBinding && changeName !== changeBinding.name) {
      // add a new property to the destructure list when a change handler is implicitly added
      // eg by assigning to a destructured property.
      getDestructurePattern(id)?.pushContainer(
        "properties",

Aha! That's the issue! In `let.ts` line 143, `translateVar` is called with `"let"` as the third parameter, while in `const.ts` line 88, `translateVar` is called without the third parameter, which defaults to `"const"`.

This means that when translating the server-side version of a `<const>` tag, the variable is declared with `const`, making it immutable. But when a function inside that `<const>` tag tries to assign to a `<let>` variable, Babel's scope tracking sees the assignment happening within the scope where the function is declared (which is in the `<const>` tag's scope), and it might be creating an issue.

Wait, let me re-read the issue more carefully. The assignment is to `timer`, which is defined by `<let>`, not to the `<const>` variable itself. So the issue is not about the `<const>` variable being immutable.

Let me look at the actual error more carefully. The user says:
> "Cannot assign to "timer" because it is a constant"

And the code is:
```marko
<let/timer=(0 as unknown as ReturnType<typeof setTimeout>)>

<const/reset=() => {
  if (timer) {
    clearTimeout(timer);
  }

  timer = setTimeout(() => {  // <-- Assignment to timer here
    input.value();
  }, input.duration);
}>
```

So `timer` is defined with `<let>`, which should make it mutable. But the error says it's a constant. This suggests that somehow Babel's scope tracking is treating `timer` as a constant.

Let me check if there's any special handling of function registration that might affect this. Looking back at the changes from 6.0.55 to 6.0.56, the function registration logic was significantly changed. In particular, the new code has a `finalizeFunctionRegistry()` function that's called at the end of `finalizeReferences()`.

   112	function couldSerializeDownstream(downstream: t.NodeExtra["downstream"]) {
   113	  if (downstream) {
   114	    return Array.isArray(downstream.bindings)
   115	      ? downstream.bindings.some((binding) => couldSerializeBinding(binding))
   116	      : couldSerializeBinding(
   117	          downstream.bindings,
   118	          downstream.excludeProperties,
   119	        );
   120	  }
   121	
   122	  return false;
   123	}
   124	
   125	function couldSerializeBinding(
   126	  binding: Binding,
   127	  excludeProperties?: Set<string> | undefined,
   128	) {
   129	  if (getBindingSerializeReason(binding.section, binding)) {
   130	    return true;
   131	  }
   132	
   133	  for (const expr of binding.downstreamExpressions) {
   134	    if (expr.isEffect || couldSerializeDownstream(expr.downstream)) {
   135	      return true;
   136	    }
   137	  }
   138	
   139	  for (const alias of binding.aliases) {
   140	    if (couldSerializeBinding(alias)) {
   141	      return true;
   142	    }
   143	  }
   144	
   145	  for (const [name, propBinding] of binding.propertyAliases) {

   147	      return true;
   148	    }
   149	  }

   209	function shouldAlwaysRegister(markoRoot: MarkoExprRootPath) {
   210	  const tag = getTagFromMarkoRoot(markoRoot);
   211	  if (!tag) return false;
   212	  if (isCoreTagName(tag, "let")) return true;
   213	  if (isCoreTagName(tag, "return")) return true;
   214	
   215	  switch (analyzeTagNameType(tag)) {
   216	    case TagNameType.DynamicTag:
   217	    case TagNameType.NativeTag:
   218	      // Passing a function to a dynamic tag could always be potentially serialized.
   219	      // Native tag event handlers are skipped in the `canIgnoreRegister`
   220	      // if it's anything else we need to unconditionally serialize.
   221	      return true;
   222	    case TagNameType.AttributeTag:
   223	      if (
   224	        analyzeTagNameType(getAttributeTagParent(tag)) ===
   225	        TagNameType.DynamicTag
   226	      ) {
   227	        return true;
   228	      }
   229	      break;
   230	  }
   231	
   232	  return false;
   233	}
   234	
   235	function getTagFromMarkoRoot(
   236	  markoRoot: MarkoExprRootPath,
   237	): t.NodePath<t.MarkoTag> | undefined {
   238	  let cur = markoRoot;
   239	  do {
   240	    if (cur.isMarkoTag()) return cur;

+export interface Input {
+  duration: number;
+  value: () => void;
+}
+
+<let/timer=(0 as unknown as ReturnType<typeof setTimeout>)>
+
+<const/reset=() => {
+  if (timer) {
+    clearTimeout(timer);
+  }
+
+  timer = setTimeout(() => {
+    input.value();
+  }, input.duration);
+}>
+
+<return=reset>
